        function getflStr(discount, rate) {
 
            var flStr = "";
            if (discount == "0") {
                flStr = "<span class=\"fl\">0</span>费率";
            }
            else if (discount && discount != "99" && parseFloat(discount) <= 4) {
 
                flStr = "<span class=\"fl\">" + (parseFloat(discount) < 4 ? parseFloat(discount) + "</span>折起" : parseFloat(discount) + "</span>折");
            }
            else {
 
                if (rate) {
                    flStr = rate == "0.00%" ? ("<span class=\"fl\">0</span>费率") : ("<span >" + rate + "</span>");
 
                }
                else {
                    //flStr = "<span class=\"fl\">0</span>费率";
                    flStr = "<span class=\"f2\">" + "---" + "</span>";
                }
            }
 
            return flStr;
        }
